All Students Immediately Withdraw

(Nanjing) Students from various universities in Shanghai petitioned the National Government to urge the government to send troops, lasting a night and a day. At 1 PM on the 27th, Zhang Zhizhong, Director of Education of the Central Military Academy, first expressed his views in a conversational manner, saying that everyone has suffered hardships and endured hunger and cold for the patriotic movement. Such perseverance and outstanding spirit will move everyone. Resisting Japan and saving the country is the urgent wish of the whole country. The government has the responsibility to defend the country and protect the people, and there is no room for shirking responsibility. In the government's measures, the environment and facts must be carefully considered. Outsiders may not fully understand, resulting in misunderstandings, and even rumors abound. Students may be impulsive due to their enthusiasm, inevitably expressing doubts, and even feeling at a loss. Now, I will briefly answer the questions raised by you to the government due to doubts as follows: (1) On the issue of assisting Ma Zhanshan, Ma's withdrawal from Heihe was not because there were no troops to assist from the rear, nor was it because he had no ability to resist the Japanese army, but because there were plainclothes teams disrupting Heihe. The Japanese army continuously bombed with airplanes. In order to protect the lives and property of hundreds of thousands of people and foreign teachers in the city, he could not bear to see the people suffer, so he had to take appropriate measures. Since September 18, the central government has been planning the affairs of the eastern provinces every day. During Ma Zhanshan's resistance against the Japanese army, there was also daily telegram exchange with the central government. To say that the central government sat idly by and did not provide assistance is to misunderstand the truth. (2) On the issue of punishing Zhang Xueliang, everything should not please the enemy and grieve the loved ones. The Japanese openly declared their opposition to Zhang Xueliang returning to the three eastern provinces. If Zhang Xueliang's power in the three eastern provinces can be eliminated, then the withdrawal of troops can be discussed. It can be seen that the Japanese are extremely opposed to Zhang Xueliang because he usually upholds national rights. Now, Zhang Xueliang should be allowed to redeem himself with merit and be responsible for recovering the lost territory. After the military situation is settled, this matter will be submitted to the judgment of the national public opinion. (3) On the issue of prohibiting student petitions, the government has always received students from all over the country who come to Beijing to petition. The purpose of the petition has also been accepted without exception. The facts in the past two months are all there. If the government does not allow students to petition, the transportation department can at any time not provide convenience. How can you come to Beijing? (4) Regarding foreign affairs, we must first seek internal unity. The government is painstakingly anxious to seek domestic peace and unification as the foundation for saving the country and resisting foreign aggression. However, recently, Guangdong has overturned the resolution of the Shanghai Peace Conference, which has created obstacles to peaceful unification and has a great impact on foreign affairs. You should understand the responsibility for undermining peaceful unification and correct it with national public opinion. Later, Chairman Chiang took the stage to give instructions, saying that the students endured hunger and cold and expressed their sincere patriotism with their perseverance and outstanding spirit, which is enough to make the enemy know the ambition and strength of our people, and should not be underestimated. He is very gratified. The wishes of the students here, if they trust the government and cooperate with the government to unanimously resist foreign aggression, will be an effective movement. If this kind of effect is lost and becomes a tool for a few people, then they themselves will have no center of gravity and strength, and can they still cope with diplomatic confrontation with the enemy? Foreigners judge the strength of China's power by the gathering and scattering of the Chinese people's spirit, the level of knowledge, and the purity and complexity of psychology. If the Chinese people are weak in knowledge and scattered in spirit, even if there are land, sea, and air forces, it will not be enough to resist the enemy. If the level is high and the strength is concentrated, even if the land, sea, and air forces are not as good as the enemy, they will not be taken advantage of by the enemy. Moreover, people bully our country and our nation because our people do not trust the government, causing the government's prestige to be swept away, and reactionary elements take the opportunity to make trouble, so that there is no way to rejuvenate both internally and externally. University students are the backbone of the intellectual class. This kind of reasoning should be understood. The students have been here for more than a day and night. Although I have not met with them immediately, I am always thinking about the suffering of my dearest youth who are enduring hunger and cold. The reason why I have not met with the students later is because I have seen points in the petition conditions that are unreasonable and exceed the norm. They cannot understand the government's painstaking efforts, and seem to express distrust of the government. Those with high knowledge and sincere patriotism should not have done this. Regarding this point, I am very heartbroken and very ashamed. I only hope that the students will make a judgment on their conscience, take a consistent attitude with the government with a pure and noble spirit, resist foreign aggression, save the country, and fight to the end. Regarding the doubts of the students about the government's measures, Director Zhang has explained them separately, and I hope you can understand. Then, the delegation replied, stating that we all have twelve points of trust in the government. This petition is purely for saving the country and is by no means manipulated by a few people. When departing, everyone made a vow, please do not misunderstand the chairman. However, because the invaders are entering deeper and the country is dying day by day, people are panicked and cannot live a day. Therefore, please ask the chairman to resolutely decide on the military and diplomatic policies to deal with the national crisis, so as to protect the integrity of the territory and comfort the hearts of the people. Chiang said that in this case, I am very gratified. I will definitely accept the requests of the students and stand in front of the people to sacrifice and fight. The delegation also asked Chiang to issue a handwritten order to express his determination to go north to recover the lost territory, so as to comfort our wishes. Chiang immediately agreed, and finally solemnly declared that he would absolutely take responsibility, do his best, and die only after exhausting his efforts. Everyone was satisfied, and there was thunderous applause. At that time, Zhang Zhizhong said that the Central Military Academy had prepared food and accommodation on behalf of the delegation, please go to rest. The handwritten order will be handed over in person after it is completed, and I will be responsible for handing it over in person. The delegation still asked to wait for the handwritten order to be issued before dispersing. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) Chiang issued a handwritten order to the Shanghai University Student Delegation Urging the Government to Send Troops, saying, "Dear students of various universities, I am deeply gratified by your patriotic enthusiasm in coming to Beijing to petition. I, the chairman, have long been determined to be loyal to the party and the country. I can accept your petition. Regarding military and diplomatic issues, Director Zhang has been sent to explain, and everyone should understand. I hope the students will tell their classmates to study with peace of mind, support the government, and do their duty." This edict, when Chairman Chiang gave instructions, the Shanghai University Delegation stated that the Shanghai Student Federation believed that the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session's denial of the Shanghai Peace Conference resolution was undermining peace and had made a serious statement, saying that in this critical diplomatic period, anyone who undermines peaceful unification is an enemy of the people. It can be seen from this that our colleagues trust the government and support peaceful unification. (Special telegram on the 27th)

(Nanjing) More than 180 students from Tsinghua University who petitioned left the National Government at 5 PM on the 27th after listening to Chairman Chiang's instructions and returned to Pingjing by crossing the river that evening. Professors of National Central University Publish a Letter to Students 23

Not Appropriate to Blame Each Other in Serious Times

Should Devote Efforts to the Intellectual Preparation for Saving the Country

(Nanjing) Professors of National Central University recently published a letter to students, saying, "Today's China, the entire country and nation, has reached an unprecedentedly serious period. Internally, natural disasters and man-made disasters occur frequently, and there are frequent disturbances. Externally, powerful neighbors send troops and national territory is occupied. In this serious period, it will not help if the Chinese people merely blame each other. Looking at the methods of various countries in dealing with national crises, none of them fail to work together to seek a unified front. Even those who are usually dissatisfied with the government, due to the national crisis, turn to do their best to support and assist it, so as to increase the strength to resist foreign aggression. Our colleagues believe that the way our country should deal with the national crisis at present has been recognized by the Chinese people, that is, to unite internally and not to yield externally. However, in order to achieve the goal of not yielding, it is by no means enough to just verbally declare war. We must have sufficient preparations in both finance and military affairs before we can talk about war. Even if we fight, we must rely on the firmness of the national spirit to be able to last. At present, it is the time for the government to strictly plan and operate. Our people across the country should calmly wait for orders, and our students across the country should temper their minds and bodies in preparation for general mobilization. However, in recent days, students from various universities have been eager to love the country and are often driven by emotions, which in turn reduces the efficiency of the government's foreign work and gives opportunities to the enemy. Is this the original intention of our youth? Our colleagues believe that the task of saving the country cannot be accomplished in a day or two. Goujian destroyed Wu, and it still required twenty years of recuperation and training. Today's wars require manpower and knowledge hundreds of times more than in the past. It goes without saying that it requires a longer period of preparation. Therefore, if our youth across the country truly take national affairs as their own responsibility, they should devote themselves to the intellectual preparation for saving the country. Such as the current strikes and abandonment of studies, running around to petition, this is truly not a good plan and is not something that our colleagues can agree with. Sincere advice, I hope you will consider it. Professors of National Central University." (Special telegram on the 27th)

Delegates Who Withdrew from the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session

Issue Two Circular Telegrams 25

Unanimously Endorsing Wang Jingwei

Accepting Encouragement to Go to the Battlefield Together

One to Various Organizations

Declaring the Truth of This Withdrawal

(Hong Kong) More than 220 delegates who withdrew from the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session issued two important telegrams. (1) To Mr. Wang Jingwei of Shanghai, I am greatly moved by reading your telegram. Since the outbreak of the Japanese invasion of the eastern provinces, the people of the whole country have been eager for unification and to die for the national crisis together. Representatives from 宁方 (Ning faction) have arrived in Guangdong one after another. Mr. Wang is anxious about foreign aggression and advocates using political solutions to replace military solutions. He spares no effort and personally participates in peace talks. Although the resolutions passed may not fully meet your intentions, your painstaking efforts to protect peace have been made clear to the world. The purpose of our trip to the south was originally to promote unification, but a small number of people are courageous in the pursuit of private interests and disregard the survival of the nation. They brazenly made a decision to undermine peaceful unification. We could not bear to see the peace that Mr. Wang had painstakingly created for several years destroyed in one fell swoop, so we resolutely withdrew together and gathered in Hong Kong. We feel the pain of the demise of the party and are also worried about the demise of the country. Our blood is boiling and we want to die without a place to die. Your telegram encourages us to join the Fourth Army and go to the battlefield together. We are moved by righteous indignation and unanimously accept it, vowing to perish together and do our best to fulfill our responsibility to save the country. A statement of grief and indignation, I hope you will consider it. (2) To all levels of party departments at home and abroad, the governments of all provinces and cities across the country, all mass organizations, and all newspapers, the purpose of the establishment of the Central Extraordinary Conference is to seek the realization of democratic politics in politics and to achieve sincere unity and seek the establishment of a democratic centralized system in the party. When the Japanese army forcibly occupied the three eastern provinces, in order to respond to the desire of the people of the whole country for peaceful unification, there was the holding of the Shanghai Peace Conference, and there was the establishment of various resolutions of the Peace Conference. The representatives carefully examined its content and the methods for resolving party affairs. Although they were unable to fully satisfy it, how could they bear to destroy peace and obstruct unification at the current time of national crisis? However, a part of the representatives of the Fourth Plenary Session, disregarding the current great disaster, resolutely overturned this resolution of the Peace Conference, causing the glimmer of hope for peaceful unification to disappear. The representatives are confident that their efforts over the years have been consistent, but they dare not agree with this reckless act that completely disregards the national interest and welfare of the people, so they withdrew from the conference together to seek a way to remedy it, and strive to realize peaceful unification. I hereby inform you and hope you will understand. Another declaration was issued, which was roughly the same as the above telegram. (Special telegram on the 27th)

Important Foreign Telegrams

French Parliament Trusts Government's Foreign Policy 47

Guomin News Agency, Paris, 27th - After midnight yesterday, the French Parliament passed a motion of confidence in Prime Minister Laval's foreign policy by a vote of 320 to 150. Laval's foreign policy

Within the framework, the payment of Allied war debts and reparations is stipulated, but in times of global financial and economic panic, temporary measures will be accepted to temporarily alleviate Germany's reparation burden as stipulated in the Young Plan. (2) France will agree that the priority of reparations can only be proportional to the reduction of France's war debts. (3) France does not agree that Germany has the right to prioritize the repayment of private debts over reparations. (4) France insists that the unconditional part of Germany's reparations should continue to be paid. France has demanded this even before the Hoover Plan, based on the above four points.

German Socialist Party's Conspiracy to Stage a Coup Discovered 48

Havas News Agency, Berlin, 26th - Yesterday, the police searched the general office of the National Socialist Party in Darmstadt and found many important documents. Prior to this, the party leader Hitler had made a solemn statement that his party members would definitely seize power without exceeding the scope of the law. This declaration has been disproved by the results of the search. The documents seized are the party's plan to stage a coup. According to news from the National Socialist Party's news agency, the party's important leaders gathered in Hesse in mid-September and drafted various documents, discussing the procedures for the coup. The general idea is that the National Socialist Party's shock troops would declare armed dictatorship, overthrowing the federal and Hesse constitutions at the same time. According to the party's central organization's long-decided plan for the transfer of administrative and legislative powers, the party's shock troops would become the police of each state after the uprising. The coup declaration drafted by the party contains an ambiguous explanation of the scope of the law. The general idea is that once those who previously held federal and state power are overthrown by the incident, a new legal status will naturally arise with the transition of the incident, similar to the overthrow of the imperial system in November 1918. Previously, a Hesse legislator named Xue Fei, who had long been at odds with the National Socialist Party, informed the police department, and the conspiracy was broken.

Another telegram states that the National Socialist Party's main organ said that this case was obviously a malicious accusation by the Social Democratic Party. The documents are all fake. The organ will publish its views on the matter as soon as it receives the necessary information and said that any party members who engage in illegal activities will be expelled from the party. The German newspaper reported that if the local coup conspiracy in Darmstadt succeeded, excessive chaos would be inevitable. No matter how this case develops, it has great significance in the changes in German domestic politics, because the attempt to unite the central party and the National Socialist Party has failed.

Opening of the International Disarmament Conference 49

Guomin News Agency, Paris, 26th - The International Disarmament Conference held its opening ceremony at the Palais des Nations today, presided over by Lord Cecil of Britain. More than 600 representatives from 17 countries and 171 organizations attended. Cecil delivered a brief opening speech, saying that competitive armament is the greatest harm to mankind. He dared to ask the people of all countries to urge their governments to eliminate this obstacle on the road to civilization. It was decided that Senator Borah, Chairman of the U.S. Senate Foreign Relations Committee, would give a radio speech across the Atlantic, advocating that all countries implement disarmament uniformly. The conference is scheduled for three days, and it is expected that many celebrities will attend the conference to give speeches. Briand hosted a banquet for the representatives this afternoon. However, Corday, a water manufacturer, posted tens of thousands of slogans throughout the city, asking the public to gather on Friday to demonstrate against the conference's unwarranted interference in France's armaments.

A landmine exploded immediately at a location two miles away from Xinmin Station, shaking the whole city. Planes dropped more than a dozen bombs near the station, and Japanese armored car soldiers opened fire at the same time, shooting at the people. Yesterday (24th) afternoon, the Japanese army covered Mongolian and Korean bandits and attacked Gaotai Tian Village, 18 miles away from Xinmin City. The county security team arrived and killed more than a dozen people, including Japanese soldiers. The bandits, seeing that the situation was not good, intended to retreat and try again. The bandits and the Japanese army then occupied the village. Wei, the magistrate of Xinmin County, negotiated with the Japanese consul, who denied any knowledge of it. At about 3:00 PM, a train of armored cars loaded with more than 100 Japanese soldiers arrived in Xinmin from Huanggu Tun and fired more than a dozen shots at the southeast of Xinmin City. The situation in Xinmin is now in a very critical state, and the scope of military operations is expanding. It is reported that another Japanese warship, the Guma, arrived in Qinhuangdao yesterday. It has a displacement of 10,000 tons and is full of wooden boxes containing munitions. When the Kailuan Mining Bureau inquired about the purpose of the ship, it was answered that it was to protect the radio station there. After the Japanese soldiers landed, more than 100 of them marched towards Shanhaiguan, obviously also with military action. The embassies stationed in Beiping recently received orders from the League of Nations to investigate the real situation in the Northeast. Yesterday, Adachi, a military attache of the British embassy, Malade, a military attache of the American embassy, Hans, a military attache of the French embassy, and Rabbi, a counselor, passed through Tianjin and went to Jinzhou one after another. It is said that the investigation time is limited to one month.

The hidden worries in Tianjin have not yet subsided. The Japanese concession is heavily guarded and very serious. After the Belgian Chamber of Commerce protested, trams were allowed to pass through the Japanese concession, but they were not allowed to stop, and the inspection was very strict. Although the shops in the Japanese concession are open, they are deserted. It is rumored that Doihara secretly came to Tianjin again yesterday, fearing that there will be another disturbance. Heilongjiang Provincial Government Moves to Hailun 54

Ma Zhanshan Safely Arrives in Eastern Heilongjiang

Zhang Jinghui Still Dares Not Go to Heilongjiang

Harbin Correspondence: Zhang Jinghui's going to Heilongjiang to take charge of the government has been determined by the Japanese army. However, the news has been circulating for three days, and Zhang has not yet set off. It is said that Zhang is concerned about his future. Although he relies on the power of the Japanese and no one dares to oppose him if he rashly goes to Heilongjiang, it is ultimately difficult to win people's hearts and rectify his name. Under the power of the Japanese army, he cannot request orders from the central government. He can only pretend to be supported by the people to preserve his face. He specially entrusted Zhao Zhongren, Li Yintang, and others from the Heilongjiang Provincial Committee to find ways to mobilize representatives of merchants and gentry in Heilongjiang to come to Harbin to invite him, and then he would go to take office. Zhao and others received the order and returned to Heilongjiang the day before yesterday to handle it. They will come to Harbin again in the next few days to urge him. It is rumored that Xi Qia will come to Harbin this week to discuss the unification of the Northeast and decide on the successor to the chief executive of the special zone. Zhang's failure to go to Heilongjiang immediately is probably to wait for Xi. Last night (21st), a Japanese colonel, on the orders of his 2nd Division Commander Domen, came to Harbin. Introduced by Japanese Consul Ohashi Tadashi, he met with Zhang in secret talks. Although it is impossible to know the inside story, it is still expected that he will still urge Zhang to go to Heilongjiang. As for the situation in Heilongjiang, it is entirely under the control of the Japanese army. Domen, the commander of the Japanese army division, has occupied the office of the deputy commander of Heilongjiang, and the military police brigade is entrenched in the provincial capital's public security bureau. In addition, the Industry Department, the Education Department, and the provincial party headquarters have also been occupied by Japanese soldiers. All telegrams and telegrams sent and received by the telephone and telegraph bureau must be checked by the Japanese. Telephone calls must be made in Japanese. Shops have not opened for three days since the Japanese army occupied the provincial capital. Yesterday, the Japanese army sent a message to the chairman of the chamber of commerce, ordering him to order the shops to open for business. Although some shops have opened, the business hours are very short, opening at 10:00 AM and closing at 3:00 PM. Food prices have skyrocketed, with each dou of grain costing 1.9 yuan and each catty of salt costing 0.3 yuan. Besides the Japanese soldiers scattered throughout the streets and merchants forced to hang Japanese flags, there are very few Chinese. Although the Qi'ang Railway's small train runs as usual every day, no passengers ride it except for Japanese soldiers. The Ta'ang Railway and the Qi'ke Railway are occupied by the Japanese army. 　The Manchukuo Railway commissioned combat workers to replace the Qi'ke Railway's cars and manage the railway from the 22nd. Another 500 people were sent to restore the Ta'ang Railway and repair the Jiang　track. Ishiwara, the former Ta'ang Railway advisor of the Manchurian Town Committee, was appointed as the director, and Wan Xianxiang, the former engineer, as the deputy director. It is scheduled to open to traffic on the first of next month. It is reported that Chairman Ma Zhanshan safely 　arrived in Hailun on the 22nd and will set up the Heilongjiang Provincial Government there to reorganize everything. However, there are no funds at present, and he hopes that all parties will provide assistance. Hailun is the terminus of the Hu-Hai Railway, and the transportation is fairly convenient. The terrain is suitable for both offense and defense. Ma's retreat to Hailun is considered a threat by the Japanese army. Several thousand cavalrymen took the Zhongxing Town route from Mingyong yesterday to attack Hailun by surprise. Therefore, a battle is likely to occur in the Hailun area soon. When Ma led his troops to retreat on the 19th, the Japanese army pursued relentlessly along the Qi'ke Railway. On the 20th, they were ambushed and defeated in Yangjiatun. The Heilongjiang army, although defeated, was still very orderly. The infantry and artillery retreated first, and the cavalry covered the rear. When they passed Yangjiatun, 500 cavalrymen were hidden in the mounds, and more than 300 militiamen and police from Tai'an Town and Keshan County were ambushed in the nearby forest. At 4:00 AM on the 20th, the Japanese cavalry chased to the ambush site. The ambush troops launched a surprise attack from three sides. The Japanese soldiers fought in panic and could not distinguish between the real and the false. Dozens were killed, and the remaining troops were shocked and retreated. The Heilongjiang army was able to retreat to Keshan calmly. At 4:00 PM on the same day, the Japanese army increased their cavalry and artillery to 2,000 and continued to pursue along the Qi'ke Railway. A fierce battle took place at Guchengzi at 9:00 PM that night. With the support of the Baiquan militia, the Japanese army was still repelled. At 10:00 AM on the 21st, two Japanese planes went to Tai'an Town and Guchengzi Station for reconnaissance and dropped six bombs on Guchengzi, destroying the ticket office and the platform. There were no battles on the Qi'ke Railway until our army retreated to Baiquan on the 21st. (November 22)

For the sake of local security, he had no choice but to fire a shot into the air to stop it. Then, because the boat still did not obey the order, he fired another shot, and the boat stopped. The militiaman boarded the boat for inspection and found that it was loaded with rice and grain, intending to smuggle it over. He immediately released it. The river surface was always calm as usual. Unexpectedly, the Japanese warship Hiraya was disturbed by itself and deliberately put on a show of panic, shining searchlights in all directions. However, the waves were as smooth as a mirror, and no gunshots were heard, so it could not display its power. It then flew to report to the Japanese consulate and sent Secretary Katsuki to the 171st Brigade of the 57th Division and the Public Security Bureau. Yan Bindu, the foreign affairs secretary of the county government, went to the Japanese consulate and met with Japanese Consul Shibasaki Hakuo to explain everything. The military and police authorities stated that the business group's firing was purely an act to maintain local security, and the Japanese side was deliberately putting on a show of panic. It is not difficult to imagine their intentions. They have now telegraphed to the higher authorities separately to report the truth. (November 25)

Jinan Prohibits Cash from Leaving the Country 56

Jinan Correspondence: After the Tianjin Incident, business was completely suspended for more than ten days. Although the market has gradually resumed trading, people are wary, and cash is accumulated and not released, and financial conditions are extremely tight. One thousand yuan of Tianjin currency is worth forty taels more than the highest time in Jinan. Even in the past one or two days, it has been more than twenty taels. The silver and money firms in Jinan believe that it is profitable, and they have been vying to transport cash to Tianjin to make profits. Within three days, a total of more than 4 million yuan was transported out. When the Pingpu train passed Jibei on the evening of the 23rd, it loaded more than 1 million yuan. A certain bank alone has already transported 500,000 yuan. (It is heard that the bank has transported more than 1 million yuan to Tianjin before and after.) Jinan is a small place, and cash reserves are limited. After this huge outflow, the market has become very dry. In recent days, those who withdraw money from silver and money firms, no matter how much, have been paid with checks, and no cash is seen. There are even those who hold checks and run around all day, pushing back and forth, and cannot get cash. If they continue to transport cash in a steady stream, Jinan's financial system will be in great panic. In view of this, the provincial government issued a ban yesterday. Last night, various silver and money firms transported tens of thousands of yuan to the Jinpu Railway Station for shipment north, but the station had already received orders to refuse loading, so they were not transported out. At 4:00 PM today, Wang Xiangrong, the director of the finance department, gathered the managers of eight banks, including the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the China Industrial Bank, the Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank, the Shandong Commercial Bank, the Zhonglu Bank, and the Continental Bank, at the Ping City Official Money Bureau, and the managers of seventeen silver firms, including Deshengchang, Juxingchang, Yuanfengcheng, Yijulong, Yijusheng, Jufeng, Jinji, Tongju, Tongheyu, Ruizengxiang, Houchang, Xiejutai, Deju, Renkang, Gongqing, Yuankang, and Yuanxing, to discuss relief measures. First, Wang reported, roughly saying that since the Northeast Incident and the Tianjin Incident occurred, financial panic has occurred everywhere. Shandong is fortunate not to have been affected. However, in recent days, due to the lack of cash in Tianjin, banks and firms in this city have been transporting cash to Tianjin. It is the duty of merchants to seek profits. This matter would be irrelevant in peacetime, but in the current situation, it must be considered. Because, unfortunately, once there is a change, the financial sector will be greatly affected. For this reason, everyone is gathered here to discuss relief methods. The Finance Department has long planned to ban the export of cash, which will be announced within one or two days. It will be canceled after the situation stabilizes. This is purely for the financial consideration of the market. I hope everyone will understand the difficulties of the times and truly express their gratitude. Next, Xu Jizhuang of the Central Bank stood up and said that Director Wang's proposal is the only way to relieve the province's financial crisis, because due to the situation, it is necessary to prepare cash, and if a large amount of cash is transported out and then transported from Shanghai, it is very difficult. If an incident occurs, those who feel pain must be from the financial community. Everyone applauded. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. It is said that the measures set by the Finance Department are that private individuals can carry up to 500 yuan of cash out of the country, and public institutions are limited to 2,000 yuan. Amounts above 2,000 yuan must state the reasons and be approved by the authorities before they can be transported out. Today, there were still those who transported cash to Tianjin on the Jinpu northbound train, and they were all ordered to unload by the Supervision Department of the Public Security Bureau. (November 25)

Disputes at Jiawang Coal Mine 58

Xuzhou Correspondence: Since the Huadong Company took over the Jiawang Coal Mine and reorganized it, coal shafts have been developed daily, and coal production has become increasingly abundant. However, the company's treatment of local farmers and workers seems to be inadequate, leading to various disputes in recent months, such as cutting down electric poles and worker strikes. The situation is recorded as follows:

Electric Pole Dispute: The Jiawang coal area is located east of the Liuquan Station of the Jinpu Railway in northern Xuzhou. The company has built the Jialiu branch line for coal transportation. The company has planted electric poles beside the branch line, within the farmers' fields. The nearby people believe that property rights have been infringed, so they organized a "Committee Against Huadong Company's Infringement of Rights" and appointed Zhu Rundong and others as representatives. In early October, they filed a complaint with the Tongshan County Government, ordering compensation for the losses. The county government ruled that infringement of property rights did not require such a large organization and should be pursued by the infringed parties. The complaint was rejected. The committee then filed a record with the county party headquarters and repeatedly negotiated with the Huadong Company. On the morning of the 19th of this month, about two or three hundred farmers from the association, each carrying a machete, cut down more than eighty electric poles near the Jialiu branch line. The Jialiu road police immediately reported to the company, which sent road patrol police to maintain order. In the evening, the farmers dispersed, and the branch line railway was preserved. According to the company's report to the county government, the former district chief Xue Yunsheng initiated this disturbance, and the current district chief Liu Jianqiu is manipulating it. The county government has ordered District Chief Liu to be responsible for prevention and not to allow the matter to escalate. The company has also reported to the Agricultural and Mining Department for protection, and the department has ordered the county government to handle the matter properly. Although this dispute has temporarily come to an end, it has not been completely resolved.

Strike Wave: The workers of the Huadong Company, because the treatment of employees is not equal and the workers mostly earn six yuan a month, which is not enough to maintain a living, raised four demands to the company in April: (1) A universal pay raise with a fixed percentage; (2) Coal transportation workers should all receive half-price benefits, and preferential treatment should not be given to officials while being stingy with workers; (3) Day and night shifts should be rotated to balance work and leisure; (4) Weekly holidays should be granted, otherwise double pay should be given. The company agreed to the first two articles, to be implemented when the company's daily coal output exceeds 400 tons. The third and fourth articles would be implemented after the promulgation of the Factory Law. In April, the daily coal output was about 300 tons. By September, the daily output had reached 500 tons, and the Factory Law was also promulgated in August. As a result, the workers reiterated their previous request, and the company agreed to consider it and respond on the 20th of this month. On the 19th, the company suddenly stopped issuing factory passes to the workers, and the workers stopped working in unison. Afterwards, the company announced that the non-issuance of worker passes was an individual error by the worker pass office clerk Qin Binfu and persuaded the workers to continue working as usual. The workers believed that the company had not yet given a satisfactory reply to the four demands and that stopping the issuance of passes was a bargaining chip, so they maintained their strike attitude and refused to resume work. The labor and management sides are gradually becoming evenly matched.

Page 10

It seems that the company is likely to be accommodating, and it may be resolved after another round of consultations. (24th)

Local gentry Zhang Yi and Pan Shengnian and others believe that the existing barracks and public places in Suzhou have long been stationed with military police and disabled soldiers. A Murdered Male Corpse Was Found Outside Panmen: A male corpse was found in the river at the Guangji Bridge mound outside Panmen on the 26th. He was about 40 years old, wearing a white undershirt on his upper body and completely naked on his lower body. His head had been chopped off, and only a few pieces of skin and flesh were still connected. It appeared to be an abandoned corpse killed due to a love affair. After the local procuratorate sent personnel to examine it, they ordered the local security to prepare a coffin for burial and sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau to arrest the murderer. However, as of the evening of the 27th, no relatives of the deceased had arrived, and there were no clues to the case.

Wuxi 61

The Entire Money Industry Was Stimulated to Suspend Business: The County Court Procuratorate, at 9:00 p.m. on the 6th of this month, acting on a secret report, searched the home of Fan Chunchen, the owner of the Defeng Money Shop on Dongda Street, for opium. At that time, Fan asked for permission to pay the fine first due to old age and illness, and he was temporarily released on bail. Recently, the Procuratorate approved the Criminal Court of the same court to send the Fan case for execution. At 9:00 a.m. on the 26th, it appointed Prosecutor Du Jiasheng to lead the bailiffs to Fan Chunchen's home to arrest him. Fan happened to be seriously ill and living in Tongren Hospital. Du and others immediately rushed to Tongren Hospital and arrested Fan and took him to the court. At the same time, Prosecutor Yang An was also sent to lead bailiffs Li Renzhen and Li Changqing to search the Defeng Money Shop opened by Fan Chunchen. They suddenly entered the silver room. When the shop saw that Yang was in plain clothes and Li and others were bald and wearing short black clothes, they asked what was happening, but they only said that they had official business and did not say their names, and they were in a hurry. They feared that they were bandits disguised as officials, so they blew the whistle and sounded the alarm. The merchant group patrol team and others went to rescue them. The neighbors around were suspicious of robbery and were extremely panicked. The order was disrupted for a time, and more and more people gathered in the street. When Yang and others realized that it was a misunderstanding, they came out proudly. The crowd did not know that they were judges and suspected that they were bandits, so they shouted loudly. Fortunately, Wang Changsheng, the captain of the merchant group patrol team, feared that an incident would occur and took Yang and others to the nearby Chamber of Commerce to inquire. Yang then said that he was a prosecutor of the court and was ordered to search Defeng and showed his search warrant in his arms. At that time, Prosecutor Du had also arrived, saying that the shop refused to be inspected and caused a dispute, and should be severely punished. After returning to the court, he immediately reported to the Chief Prosecutor Zhou Erkai and telegraphed the situation to the High Court. The Money Industry Association also convened an emergency meeting, believing that the current situation was unstable and that bandits often impersonated officials to search and rob. The case of the Jiangsu Bank robbery in broad daylight the year before could serve as a lesson. In today's Defeng case, Prosecutor Yang did not state his name or the details of the case in advance, and suddenly entered the silver room for inspection, which was enough to make the industry feel cold. They must seek official guarantees for their business in order to ensure safety. It was unanimously decided to suspend business on the 27th and wait for a solution. That night, they also telegraphed the High Court, requesting that Yang An be dismissed. At the same time, they submitted petitions to the county government and the court, requesting relief. Yesterday (27th), all 18 money shops in the city suspended business. The County Chamber of Commerce, as well as China, Communications, Jiangsu, Shanghai, Industry, Continent, Farmers, and other banks, also urgently telegraphed the High Court, requesting a prompt and fair trial to protect the commercial market and maintain the rule of law. County Magistrate Chen Hua and the Director of the Public Security Bureau also invited Yang, the President of the County Court, and the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce to persuade the money industry to resume business immediately and wait for a solution to maintain the market.

Gamblers Refuse Arrest and Beat Police: According to a secret report from the County Government, there were gambling activities in Shitangwan. It immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to send police to the countryside to investigate and arrest. More than 30 gamblers were arrested in the two gambling dens, Huifang Garden opened by Qin Afa and the home of Liu Asan. At that time, the gamblers were engrossed in gambling. When they saw the police arrive, they relied on their numbers and shouted loudly, and removed the wooden bridges before and after the town. Some policemen were beaten into the river, and some had their uniforms torn. Fortunately, Wang, the platoon leader of the railway protection soldiers at the station, heard the alarm and led his soldiers to suppress the situation, and the siege was relieved. The gamblers Shen Fulin, Wang Along, Biao Xiangfa, Zhu Xifeng, Biao Changsheng, Wang Debiao, and Lu Luzi were escorted to the city and interrogated by Fu Hongsheng, the section chief of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau. Each of them denied gambling and beating the police. They were ordered to be sent to the County Court for trial.

Jiangyin 62

Shanghai Detectives Arrive in Cheng to Arrest Buyers of Stolen Goods: In August of this year, the Texaco Company of the United States hired Xu Shaoqing and Li Changsheng, boatmen from Yancheng, through Qian Mingrong, the owner of the shipping company, to transport 1,000 boxes of Xingfu brand kerosene to the Hangzhou Zhakou branch for unloading. Unexpectedly, the boatmen transported the kerosene to Jiangyin and secretly contacted Fan Guijin from Jingjiang, selling 500 boxes to Yuan Taichang outside the North Gate (two boxes were later returned), agreeing on a price of 5 yuan and 5 jiao per box (the original price was 9 yuan and 7 jiao and a half). Fan received a commission of one silver yuan per box, and paid 1,250 yuan at the time, agreeing to pay 500 yuan on the 15th of the lunar October and 1,000 yuan on the 10th of the lunar December. The kerosene had been sold. The remaining 500 boxes were sold to a certain place in Huangdu. After receiving a letter from Zhakou, the company learned of the situation and reported it to Chen Xizeng, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, who sent Detective Captain Lu Ying to arrest the boatman Xu Shaoqing. Yesterday (26th), a formal document was sent to the county government, and detectives Chen Caifu, Zhao Huairen, Wang Xingao, and others were sent to the county government to submit the document and arrest Yang Qiming, the owner of Yuan Taichang, and Fan Guijin, the introducer. Many empty kerosene boxes were seized. Wu, the auditing officer, clarified the case in the evening. As the case still required investigation, he refused to take the suspects to Shanghai. The Chamber of Commerce defended Yang for mistakenly buying stolen goods. The court ordered him to be released on bail. The detectives returned to Shanghai on the 27th to report.

Nantong 63

Suppressing the Harassment of Salt Smugglers in Jiangbei: Recently, in various counties north of the Yangtze River, salt smugglers from Yancheng and Funing and other places have colluded with bandits, using the name of escaping famine to cause serious harassment. The province has ordered the counties along the Yangtze River and the sea to send police teams to suppress and block them.

Yangzhou 64

The Anti-Japanese Association's Statement After the Resolution of the Strike: The industry and commerce have resolved the strike caused by the investigation and punishment of Japanese goods in this city. Now, I learned that the Anti-Japanese Association reported that the strike had been resolved by the Provincial Committee. However, the association had not received any orders from the County Party Department, nor had it received a formal request from the Chamber of Commerce. The association made an urgent statement yesterday (26th), stating that it has the right to weigh and measure all issues related to the handling of sealed Japanese goods in the future.

Shops That Were Punished Have Not Yet Opened: The dispute between the strike by merchants and the Anti-Japanese Association in this city has been resolved by the Provincial Committee. Yesterday (25th), all shops opened for business as usual. However, the Kaitai Fu and other shops that were previously punished by the Anti-Japanese Association have not yet opened, and the words "This shop is closed, and all employees are not working" are written on the door. It is reported that the cigarette holders imported by Kaitai Fu have been sent to Shanghai, and the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association has 行 别 confirmed that they were produced by the German company Huazhang, and not Japanese goods. The evidence was sent to the Chamber of Commerce last night for submission to the County Party Department for review, requesting punishment for the Anti-Japanese Association's improper handling of the situation.

Gaoyou 65

The Director of the Busy Cao Bureau Was Detained: Feng Jinyang, the former director of the Busy Cao Bureau of the County Finance Bureau, engaged in private fraud. Cao, a former grain clerk, accused him of this to the County Government. Magistrate Li said that he had repeatedly ordered him to submit the account books for the 17th, 18th, and 19th years, but he had not yet submitted them, which showed that the fraud was real. Yesterday, he specially sent the police to arrest Feng and temporarily hand him over to the Public Security Section for detention.

Qingjiang 66

Nanxinji Was Robbed by Bandits: Nanxinji in Siyang, about 60 miles southwest of the county seat, is connected to the territory of the Second District of Huaiyin. Yesterday (20th), six or seven hundred bandits arrived in the town, falsely claiming to be government troops being reorganized, passing through the town, and would leave after lunch. The locals believed it was true. Only the county police team of about 50 people stationed there and the security group Dong Chen Peihua and others saw that their actions were suspicious, but they were afraid that they were outnumbered. They avoided the area in advance. At 1:00 p.m., the bandits began to loot wildly. Almost no merchant or resident in the entire town was spared. Finally, dozens of people were kidnapped.

Jiaxing 67

The Director of the County Public Security Bureau Was Replaced: Gao Derun, the director of the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau, was reported to the province by local people for condoning his subordinates and receiving illegal fees. After the Civil Affairs Department sent personnel to investigate, Gao was transferred to the province, and Xu Yanhua was appointed to replace him. Xu arrived in He on the 26th to take over.

The Director of the Finance Bureau Solicited Public Bonds: Xu Fanzhao, the director of the Jiaxing County Finance Bureau, was ordered by the Finance Department to go to Jiashan, Chongde, Tongxiang, Haiyan, Pinghu, and other counties formerly under the jurisdiction of Jiaxing to actively raise funds for the provincial clearing of old debt bonds. Xu set off to various counties on the 27th to actively solicit donations.

Hangzhou 68

A Large Batch of Red Pill Raw Materials Was Seized in Jianggan: Toxic substances are spreading throughout Xidong, and their source is transported from Shanghai to Hangzhou. At about 5:00 a.m. yesterday, Han Yongpei, a policeman from the Second Sub-district of the Fourth District, saw a boatman, Wang Jianghong, carrying a burlap bag on his shoulder, looking flustered. He was immediately detained for inspection. It turned out to be 12 large cloth packages of red pill raw materials, made of heroin and morphine, weighing 36 jin, worth more than 2,000 silver dollars. He was escorted to the dock, and the boat owner Wu Shicun was arrested and taken to the police station. He confessed that Xu Jinxing from No. 36 Fumiaoqian had entrusted him to transport the materials to Lanxi. A document was prepared and sent to the court for trial.

Clearing of Old Debt Bonds Will Be Repaid: The eleventh drawing for the repayment of the principal of Zhejiang's old debt bonds was held on the 25th. The winning numbers were 02, 15, 28, 36, 44, 55, 67, 81, 88, and 97, a total of ten numbers. The repayment of the principal will begin on December 1st by local banks in China and county governments, along with the issuance of interest once. It is reported that the total amount of principal repayment and interest issuance is 392,400 yuan. The original fund income (increase in the price of salt) is far from sufficient. The Finance Department has allocated 140,000 yuan, which is still short by about 50,000 yuan. Other methods are being sought to raise the funds. This public bond was originally scheduled to be repaid in twelve installments. The next repayment period is on June 1st next year. The remaining numbers (the last two digits of the bond face value) are only 04, 17, 18, 38, 47, 62, 69, and 85, a total of eight numbers.

Ningbo 69

The County Government Borrowed 200,000 Yuan from Merchants: Since the Yin County Government took over the city government, its expenses have been extremely stretched. Not only is there no construction fee, but also the regular expenses for public security, education, and other items have been in arrears for several months. Therefore, it borrowed 200,000 yuan from various businesses. It has now been completed. More than 20,000 yuan in arrears for public security fees were paid in full yesterday. The arrears for education fees will be paid today. The remaining funds will be kept under the management of a management committee for construction purposes.

Yesterday afternoon, a sudden group of more than 20 bandits robbed the four or five rifles owned by the security team. Afterwards, they went to the Sanyangtai commercial store and Xiangfeng rice mill, looting a total of more than 300 yuan. The neighboring village of Shijiatang, the Bi Yongjiang Guanqi store, and the Bi Aga and other five families were also robbed by bandits, losing 500 or 600 yuan. Bi Fuju, the owner of Yonglong store, was also injured. In the evening of yesterday, five robbers broke into the home of Li Caifa, a businessman in Houtang River in western Yin, and looted gold jewelry, clothing, and other items, losing 300 to 400 yuan.

The Ministry Urges the Submission of Information on Literacy Campaigns 71

Dissemination of Comparative Status Reports on Literacy Campaigns Already Held in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing

The Ministry of Education distributed a booklet comparing the literacy campaign propaganda held in the three provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing, and issued a notice to the education departments of the provinces and cities that had not yet submitted reports, stating that literacy campaigns are of great importance. The Ministry has long formulated and promulgated the "Outline of the Literacy Campaign Propaganda Plan" for implementation. In recent years, many provinces and cities have followed the outline and actively promoted it. Among them, the three provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing have achieved the most remarkable results. Jiangsu Province's detailed planning and diligent implementation are particularly commendable. In order to facilitate reference by various provinces and cities, we have compiled a comparison of the literacy campaign propaganda held in the three provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing based on the original reports submitted by the three provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing in previous years. It is printed into a special booklet and distributed with this order. We hope that provinces and cities that have already organized and achieved results will continue to work hard on the existing foundation to ensure the early success of the literacy campaign and become a model for the whole country. Those provinces and cities that have not yet submitted reports or organized campaigns should refer to the items listed in the booklet and organize them immediately to promote progress. After the campaign is organized, you should submit the most recent information on the organization and specific plans for assessment as soon as possible. This is of utmost importance. This order.

Tangwan People's Education Center 82

The programs included: (1) Beggars Save the Country; (2) Eliminating Superstition Through Mining; (3) Patriotic Youth. The performances were vivid and colorful, and won the sympathy of the audience. It is said that no fewer than 5,000 people watched that day.

Free Talk

Reminiscences of the Diaoliang 93

-- Swallow

The Japanese pirates of Jiaqing in the Ming Dynasty. What is recorded in the historical records is only the general outline. The notes of various families have also failed to detail them. The Zhou family of Fengxian were descendants of Lord Zhongjian of the Song Dynasty. They lived as a clan, numbering about hundreds of households. Among them was General Zhou Yongwei, whose residence, Jiawei, had assets worth millions of gold. The elegance of the garden and cups was unparalleled at the time. When the Japanese pirates invaded Puzuo, they burned his garden. Zhou was so grieved and indignant that he destroyed his family to relieve the disaster, gathering local militias and training them into elite troops day and night. The following year, the Japanese pirates came again. Zhou invited them to fight, and countless were killed. The Japanese pirates retreated in defeat, hoisting their sails and leaving. Zhou anticipated that they would come for revenge, so he built defensive fortresses everywhere and guarded them day and night. Qi Jiguang reported his war performance to the court. By imperial decree, he was conferred the title of General Yongwei and subordinated to Qi's command. Thus, the troops were well-equipped and trained more diligently. Before long, the Japanese pirates indeed invaded in large numbers. Qi and Zhou ambushed them at Jinshan Hui and the Huijie area, capturing and beheading the Japanese chieftain. From then on, the Japanese pirates dared not cross the Lei Pond one step. Critics all said that Zhou's war achievements, although initially motivated by righteous indignation, would not have been known or recorded without Qi Jiguang's commendation. Compared with the present time, when General Ma is fighting alone with loyalty and bloodshed and no one comes to his aid, the difference is incalculable. I humbly hope that the authorities will rise up like General Qi and not let their ambition fall.

Chatting in the Studio Where the Weeds are Not Removed -- By Zhai Fu

The Process of Starving to Death 94

This year's flood victims, according to the Water Disaster Relief Committee, numbered as many as 50 million, and those who starved to death were counted in the millions. The inaugural issue of Anhui Disaster Weekly contains an article by He Ming describing the process of "starving" to "death," which is unbearable to read. But it is necessary to present it to the people of the country, hoping that those who have food to eat during this national crisis will not forget the compatriots in the flood-stricken areas who have no food to eat. He Yiming's report is:

"The process of 'starving' to 'death' is very simple. First, the body becomes weak and can still speak in a low voice. Further on, one can no longer speak, but the legs can still move. At this stage, if one falls asleep peacefully and does not move, one can prolong the agony for quite some time. If there is an ignorant son or daughter crying for food beside you, or if you can't bear to see your children starve in the same way, and you try to crawl elsewhere to get something for your children to eat, then as soon as you exert yourself, a stream of yellow water will flow from your mouth, and your body will fall to the ground with this stream of yellow water, never to move again. Every person who starves to death inevitably has to emit this stream of yellow water; every person who emits yellow water due to starvation inevitably dies instantly. Yellow water, it is forever imprinted in my mind!"

Wu Zhilao's Personal Humiliation by the Japanese 95

— Zheng Yimei

Mr. Wu Zhihui, a prominent figure in the Party-State, was unconventional and carefree. His morality and wit were beyond the reach of ordinary people. He was truly the Dongfang Manqian of the Republic of China era. Mr. Wu admired simplicity and frugality, not caring about his attire. He would walk through the streets. I still remember one evening this summer, I saw him strolling leisurely on Nanjing Road, appearing very relaxed, probably taking a walk after dinner. Suddenly, two or three playful young people on the left side of the road, who also recognized Mr. Wu, called out "Wu Zhihui" in strange voices repeatedly. Mr. Wu, hearing the voices, suspected they were violent people who might be harmful to him. He immediately rushed into a nearby fruit and snack shop, using the purchase of food as an excuse to avoid them. It was wise to protect himself, which was reasonable. He loved reading tabloids and supplements in various newspapers, often selecting and buying them from newsstands. In his early years, he also enjoyed writing fictional stories. The book "Talking About Ancient and Modern Times" was a monumental work that used the format of a novel to expound on scientific principles. He was skilled at creating楹聯 (楹聯 a pair of scrolls with antithetical sentences, usually displayed on both sides of a doorway). Those who sought them were numerous and insistent, which Mr. Wu found troublesome. He once described his own calligraphy as "dog scratches and cat footprints," defiling white paper. Such was his humor and humility. This time, with the Japanese acting recklessly, Mr. Wu felt particularly indignant. A guest who knew some of his anecdotes said that years ago, when Mr. Wu was traveling in Japan, he had personally suffered humiliation from the Japanese. When he was tipsy, he would often talk about it himself. It happened in the twenty-eighth year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty (the thirty-fifth year of Meiji in Japan). Mr. Wu and Mr. Sun Bojun strongly requested the ambassador to send students to study at public schools. This incurred the jealousy and anger of the authorities. The Japanese police department then deported Mr. Wu and Mr. Sun back to their hometowns to humiliate them. After Mr. Wu was arrested, he believed that a scholar could be killed but not humiliated. He wanted to awaken the masses through his death. Thus, when the police officers were escorting him out of the country, he jumped into the river to join Qu Yuan (a famous Chinese poet who drowned himself in a river). Fortunately, he was rescued. A friend found a letter in his clothes with the words "His words are good" on the cover. The letter inside read: "Believe in it unto death, make it clear not to be a traitor. Civil rights and freedom, the law of the nation. Cutting hair for innovation, a single word can decide. Use the corpse as remonstrance, worry about the crooked chimney. Alas, how sorrowful! What does the ambassador have to do with it? Confucius said to achieve benevolence, Mencius said to take righteousness. The misery of national demise will be like this. Gentlemen, work hard. I will never die." The words were passionate and慷慨 (kāng kǎi, deeply moved), comparable to Wen Tianxiang's "Song of Righteousness," both shining brightly through the ages.

Notes on Overseas Current Affairs Cartoons Seen 96

— Lü Bing

The invading Japanese army has invaded our Northeast Three Provinces, forcibly occupying land and massacring our people. The situation is serious and has shocked the world. Therefore, many magazines sent from Europe and the United States mention the Sino-Japanese incident. There are also some cartoons that subtly satirize it. After flipping through them, I will briefly describe one or two to show the observations of overseas people on the Japanese military annexation, which are quite different.

Last month's British women's magazine had a cartoon depicting an Eastern man and a Chinese woman standing side by side, looking like a quarreling couple. In the middle is a child, with the words "South Manchurian Railway" written on it, looking like he is covering his face and crying. Behind the Chinese woman is another woman, referring to Russia, implying support. The display of the picture is like this. Whether it is reasonable, the readers can probably see it. The Japanese army is not acting this time for the South Manchurian Railway; in fact, it wants to annex our country by force. Our country is united from top to bottom, sharing the same hatred of the enemy. Justice still exists, and there will eventually be a day of victory. There is no need for Russian help, and Russia may not be able to help us. If the Northeast Three Provinces incident can be compared to a couple's quarrel, and the South Manchurian Railway is regarded as a child between the two parties, it is even more inconsistent with the facts and reason.

The American "Mirror" newspaper has also recently published a cartoon, depicting two children fighting to light firecrackers. On the firecrackers is labeled "World War." Americans already know that the Northeast Three Provinces incident cannot be resolved satisfactorily and may lead to a world war. But they also know that our country did not want to set off this terrible firecracker, and tried its best to avoid its ignition. If unfortunately it explodes, it will be the Japanese who light it with fire. Therefore, saying that Chinese people and Japanese people are fighting to set off the firecrackers of World War is not as reasonable as saying that the Japanese set it off alone.

The Anti-Japanese Hero Jian Dashī 97

— Ms. Wang Junfang

I remember years ago, I read Mr. Shoujuan's small book "Violet Flowers" at a friend's place. There was an article in it describing the anti-Japanese experiences of the Taiwanese hero Jian Dashi. His heroism and greatness are enough to inspire our people to fight for the country. Now I will describe what I can remember to encourage the people of the country.

In the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, our country was defeated by Japan. Japan wanted to obtain the Northeast Three Provinces, but Li Hongzhang resisted it strongly without success. In the end, Taiwan was ceded for peace. At that time, the Taiwanese people heard of this and rose up in opposition, repeatedly appealing to the Qing court without success. Among the major clans in Taiwan, there was a person named Jian Dashi, who was not well-read but was naturally chivalrous and quite popular. He heard that the Qing court was about to hand over Taiwan, and angrily said, "Is it not possible to resist with force? Those who are noisy and like to be superior to others in peacetime are afraid when things happen, they are not real men." Those who heard his words were all moved and united, vowing to resist Japan to the death. Dashi then summoned his comrades and joined the Black Flag Army Liu Yongfu to actively prepare for war. When Japanese warships came to attack, they triggered a water mine and were lost, killing dozens of Japanese soldiers. The Taiwanese people cheered and the sound shook the sky. Japan dispatched more than forty armored cruisers from across the country, and besieged them again. Dashi led the strong men in a bitter battle, and drove women to farm, holding out for many years without running out of food. Later, due to insufficient ammunition, he took money across the Min River to purchase military supplies to replenish it. However, most of it was captured by the Japanese, or sent by Chinese officials tied up on Japanese warships to curry favor with the enemy. Thus, there was no way to hold out. They held on until after August of the tenth month when Taiwan fell. However, there were still street battles for several days. When strength was exhausted and support was cut off, he disguised himself and fled to the Min River, thinking of making another attempt. Unfortunately, he was betrayed by a friend, and the Min official tied him up and sent him to Taiwan. The Japanese imposed extreme punishment on him. When he was executed, Taiwanese people left their houses to watch. They saw their anti-Japanese leader's intestines flow out and blood fly, and everyone lowered their heads and wept, unable to bear to watch. After that, the Taiwanese people gave up the idea of ​​restoring their homeland and fell into slavery. I remember that Dashi used the small land of Taiwan to resist the national army of Japan for more than a year without surrendering. Although Taiwan was lost, it cannot be said that there was no one. Compared to the Battle of the Yellow Sea, Japan lost our Beiyang Fleet in just one day, which is even more heroic for Dashi.

Short News: Calligrapher Zhang Zhenlü grieves that General Ma Zhanshan's isolated army has been lost, and still inspires the patriotic spirit of a Confucian scholar. He donates paper and ink to write couplets to raise money to support his counterattack. Anyone who donates more than one yuan or more will be given a five-foot couplet. It is handled by the North Army Road Liangchen Hao Youshe (a friendly society). There is a declaration printed, with slogans such as "Devote yourself to the cause until death, what harm is there in breaking your wrist? Wielding a pen is as good as facing a thousand soldiers. Gathering bits of fur makes a strong fortress," "See the unanimous approval of the people and their virtues, and lead the government's deployment of troops," etc. It is very passionate and righteous. There will probably be many sympathizers.

World Snippets 98

— Hai Ke

Two Hearts. Recently, a female baby died in East Ham, England. After death, the doctor dissected the body and found an unprecedented miracle. It turned out that she had two hearts in her chest cavity. However, only one heart was active on weekdays. The other heart was still there.

Radio Little Star. The United States is the world's number one in radio fever. Among the radio stars, there is a youngest girl named Theresa McKinty, who is only two and a half years old this year. But she can recite 209 poems on the radio, including French and Italian. The tones are sonorous and very moving. It is said that she was broadcasting on the radio at the age of two.

Mobile Dancing Floor. The British White Star Shipping Company recently installed a detachable mobile dancing floor in the dining room of its "Majestic" ship. The area is 425 square feet. It is made of 236,940 pieces of oak, walnut, mahogany, maple, rosewood, and other plywood, backed with canvas. When not in use, it can be rolled up and put aside.

Heroic Literature (3) 99

— Tian You

When the Treaty of Shimonoseki was concluded, our country ceded Taiwan to Japan. The Taiwanese people strongly opposed it, so they organized a republic and elected Governor Tang Jingsong as president to resist Japan. That was a dramatic act with sound and color. The passionate and heroic situation is written so vividly that you can see it.

"The drums rumble loudly on the city wall. "Heaven, Heaven!! Tears fall like rain!! The Japanese are actually ceding Taiwan away. In the beginning, the territory was included in the treasure house of heaven. Heaven felt it from afar and reached the land where the sun rises. My great-grandfather, grandfather, and father killed the weeds and came to this land. Sugar, tea, and snow, thousands of billions of trees. Annual taxes, countless gold and money. Why does Heaven abandon me? Why is Heaven angry? Taking my fat and ointment to share with the enemy. That greedy and insatiable rat. What crime have the people committed to suffer this hardship? Who destroyed Qin? Three households of Chu. What's more, there are millions of households in Fujian and Guangdong. Everyone will fight to the death and swear to resist. With the unity of all the people, who dares to insult us? Success or failure, benefit or harm is not what we see."

With a shout, he drew his sword and struck the pillar. "There is nothing else to say today. Whoever does not obey, I will kill you with my own hands."

The glorious blue flag stands with a yellow tiger. The whole city crowds to watch, the streets empty and dancing. A golden,斗大 (斗大 dǒu dà, as big as a dou (a unit of dry measure)) seal is tied with a rope. They directly call the governor the president. "Today's government is for the people. Tainan and Taipei are our strongholds. Do not step over the雷池 (léi chí, Lei Chi, a forbidden area)."

The above is the enthusiastic anti-Japanese situation within five minutes. The following describes the result.

"The wind howls angrily in Haicheng in May. Three hundred golden-winged ships fly here. Pursuing the giant ships like a tide. Those who land first are fierce tigers. Those who seize the pass later are flying monkeys. The guns and Bizen knives in front of the village. They are defeated and the blood flows. The gods are burned and the ghosts are rotten, the city gate burns. Who will fight and defend? Who can escape?"

"A round of red sun is high in the sky. Thousands of white flags flutter in the wind. The gentry and elders invite each other. Kneeling on both sides of the road, bowing and bowing. Red tassels, bamboo hats, brocade scarves. Green silk braids hanging down like clouds. Kneeling and holding a silver plate with tea and pastries. Silk-embroidered gourds and purple grapes. "General, you have come from afar, you must be tired. The surrendered people respectfully treat the general." The general said, "Come, call your Cao. You and I are of the same race and originally compatriots. Koxinga was a hero among men. He opened up this land to divide the茅 (máo, weeds). Today, return me to the Tianshi sect. The country is as benevolent and holy as Yao. Nurturing you and educating you are different from the Li Miao. Secure your homes and families, no quarrels."

The general walked slowly, the dust did not disturb. Ten thousand horses entered the city, the wind whistling. Alas, the general is not a heavenly pride. The power of the royal army is all-encompassing. We place our lives in the hands of the general. How dare we not return to the enlightened and holy dynasty?"

At that time, with all of China fighting against Japan, there was still the defeat of the Jiawu year. It was originally an extremely difficult thing to resist Japan with Taiwan Province alone. But the enthusiasm of the previous day and the listless surrender of today is too embarrassing. Therefore, Gongdu sighed and ended the story.

"Alas, oh! How sad! All of you in Taiwan. Why were you so loyal and brave yesterday, and so cowardly today? Everything is fickle and changes with the blink of an eye. There is no preparation for war and defense in peacetime. Loyalty and righteousness are unreliable."

Rotary Club Storytelling

A Country Bumpkin Comes to Shanghai Again (30) 100

— Bao Tianxiao

But he felt something was strange: it was not yet very late, about seven or eight o'clock, why were the night watchmen already out? Or because the times were bad, there was a curfew early on, and pedestrians had to be cut off at eight or nine o'clock, so the watchmen naturally had to come out. But I heard that Shanghai was the safest place, so when the mainland encountered turmoil, everyone ran to Shanghai. Could it be that I have come to Shanghai with difficulty, and I am encountering a curfew period again?

He looked closely and felt even more wrong. Why are these watchmen young, and there are even very young and beautiful women among them? Of course, these can only be called watchwomen, and can no longer be called watchmen. Or have the old watchmen been unable to strike the watch, and passed it on to their children? The watchmen who strike the watch also hold a small flag in their hands, which is a very novel trick.

They gradually walked from that table to this table.

"Since they are striking the watch, they should strike it on the road, why are they walking into the house?" The country bumpkin was even more puzzled.

They stepped forward, first bowed to the country bumpkin, and then gave him a flyer-like piece of paper. There were many words on the paper, and although the country bumpkin also knew a few words, he did not dare to look at the flyer. Don't look at him as a coarse person, he is also careful in his coarseness. Someone once told him: "Shanghai is the most dangerous place. If someone gives you a piece of paper when you are walking on the road, you must not take it. Because there are often communists and reactionaries spreading leaflets there. The person who distributes the leaflets knows that they are dangerous goods and runs away quickly. You take his leaflet, and you don't even know what is written on it? The detectives see you holding the leaflet in your hand, and they will arrest you. I heard that a country bumpkin came and was walking on the road, and saw a newspaper on the ground. He picked it up and thought it was very clean, and it would be useful to wrap his shoes. So he wrapped a pair of broken shoes in the newspaper and went to the train station, but was detained by the police, who said that he was carrying contraband. He couldn't figure out what the contraband was? Who knew that the newspaper wrapping the shoes was a reactionary newspaper. The country bumpkin couldn't figure out what a reactionary was, but he suffered in court." In this situation, people regard Shanghai as a dangerous abyss.

Now the country bumpkin sees the watchmen also handing out flyer-like pieces of paper, and he remembers the story that people told him, and he no longer dares to look at it.

"Sir! We are all students in the school, out to solicit donations for flood relief. Please look at the faces of the flood victims and donate some money. No matter how much, it is good." The two students who were soliciting donations for flood relief for the first time spoke very gently.

Commercial News

Finance 101

Gold Price Drops Nine Taels

Large Fluctuations with a Difference of Over Twenty Taels. Yesterday, the price of gold suddenly showed signs of weakness, changing rapidly and with great volatility. There was a difference of as much as twenty taels between the morning and evening, causing panic. In the end, the calculated drop was around nine taels. Most of the damage was to internal transactions. The initial market was relatively stable, slightly rising, and unaffected by external news. However, due to the weakening of foreign exchange rates, it tended to soften, fluctuating around 70 taels. At noon, bad news suddenly spread that the situation in the north was deteriorating, with rumors of Jinzhou being in danger. This further weakened the market. Later, the market suddenly broke through 660 taels, with selling pressure surging, almost like a river flowing downwards. Foreign exchange bills also became scarce, and Indian rupee telegraphic transfers also rose. However, buyers appeared to be more active later, and the falling trend subsided, and it recovered to over 60 taels. In short, the chaotic state makes it difficult to predict the trend.

The Morning Market is Still Flat, Before the Closing Plunge. The market opened slightly higher by 1.8 taels, at 673.5 taels. Large bars rose by only one-eighth. American banks were closed for holidays and there was no telegraph. Buyers were relentless and the price rose to 75 taels. However, Yuanmao, Yongheng, Changyong, Fushunli, Wanxing, etc. were selling, and British gold banks initially entered at 75, but then settled. The US dollar was also doing 32.6875 yuan, and the price of gold fell by 7 taels. There was a fluctuation of 2 taels in a moment, until the British gold announcement released 25 basis points, and it became 66.5 taels.
